📄 ARCHIVO 1: 02_SIMULATION_MODEL/06_Corrugator.md
# 06 – Corrugator
# INGETRANS Reel Loading Simulator V4

## Propósito
Línea de producción de cartón corrugado. Es el "sumidero" del sistema: consume papel de los roll stands a velocidad variable, produce metros lineales de cartón, y es el principal generador de OEE, producción real y eventos de starvation/failure.

## Entradas
- Reels disponibles en los roll stands (paper grades)
- Órdenes de producción (Production Orders)
- Parámetros de velocidad (m/min)
- Eventos de fallo (Failures)

## Salidas
- Producción en metros lineales (live KPI)
- Consumo de papel (en kg y m²)
- OEE calculado en tiempo real
- Eventos de starvation, failure, slowdown

## Configuración
Ver `03_CONFIG_DATABASE/config_corrugator.yaml`

## Dependencias
- Depende de: RollStand, Reel, ProductionOrder, PaperGrade, Failure
- Consumida por: KPI Engine, Financial Engine, Animation Engine

## Validación
- speed ∈ [0, max_speed]
- production ≥ 0
- availability ∈ [0, 100]
- OEE = A × P × Q

## KPIs afectados
- **OEE** (principal)
- **Availability**
- **Performance**
- **Quality**
- **Throughput (m/h)**
- **Production Real vs Teórica**
- **Starvation Events**
- **Downtime %**

## Riesgo
- **Crítico**: fallos de corrugadora = pérdida directa de producción

## Prioridad
- **Crítica** — Es el corazón de la planta

---

## Atributos

| Atributo | Tipo | Unidad | Default | Min | Max | Obligatorio |
|---|---|---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| corrugator_id | str | - | "CORR-01" | - | - | Sí |
| max_speed | float | m/min | 350 | 100 | 500 | Sí |
| average_speed | float | m/min | 220 | 100 | 350 | Sí |
| current_speed | float | m/min | 0 | 0 | max_speed | Sí |
| min_speed | float | m/min | 50 | 0 | 100 | Sí |
| status | str | - | "idle" | - | - | Sí |
| paper_width_mm | float | mm | 2500 | 1800 | 3500 | Sí |
| paper_grade_active | PaperGrade | - | null | - | - | No |
| current_order | ProductionOrder | - | null | - | - | No |
| total_produced_m | float | m | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| total_produced_good_m | float | m | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| total_produced_waste_m | float | m | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| time_running_s | float | s | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| time_idle_s | float | s | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| time_failed_s | float | s | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| time_starved_s | float | s | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| time_slowdown_s | float | s | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| time_planned_s | float | s | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| setup_time_s | float | s | 1200 | 300 | 3600 | Sí |
| cleaning_time_s | float | s | 1800 | 600 | 3600 | Sí |

---

## Estados (State Machine)

IDLE → SETUP → RUNNING → CHANGING_REEL → RUNNING ↓ SLOWDOWN (speed < avg) ↓ STARVED (no reel) ↓ FAILED ↓ REPAIRING ↓ MAINTENANCE ↓ CLEANING


### Diagrama completo de transiciones
| Desde | Evento | Hacia | Condición |
|---|---|---|---|
| IDLE | order_received | SETUP | orden lista |
| SETUP | setup_complete | RUNNING | elapsed ≥ setup_time |
| RUNNING | reel_low | CHANGING_REEL | remaining < threshold |
| CHANGING_REEL | change_complete | RUNNING | - |
| RUNNING | speed_drop | SLOWDOWN | speed < avg_speed * 0.8 |
| SLOWDOWN | speed_recover | RUNNING | speed ≥ avg_speed * 0.8 |
| RUNNING | no_reel | STARVED | todos los stands vacíos |
| STARVED | reel_arrived | CHANGING_REEL | - |
| * | failure_detected | FAILED | random() < failure_prob |
| FAILED | repair_complete | RUNNING o IDLE | - |
| * | maintenance_window | MAINTENANCE | - |
| MAINTENANCE | maint_complete | IDLE | - |
| * | cleaning_window | CLEANING | elapsed ≥ 16h |
| CLEANING | cleaning_complete | IDLE | - |

---

## Inputs
1. Production Order recibida → ORDER_START
2. Reel disponible en stand → REEL_READY
3. Reel running low → REEL_CHANGING
4. Failure detectada → FAILURE
5. Maintenance programado → MAINTENANCE_START
6. Speed command (operador) → SPEED_CHANGE

## Outputs
1. **Producción en m** (live KPI cada segundo)
2. **Consumo de papel** (kg/h, m²/h)
3. **Eventos**: ORDER_STARTED, ORDER_COMPLETED, REEL_CHANGED, FAILURE_OCCURRED, REPAIR_COMPLETED
4. **OEE live** (A × P × Q recalculado cada 60s)
5. **Alertas**: STARVATION, FAILURE, SLOWDOWN
6. **Métricas de turno**: producción, OEE, disponibilidad

---

## Relaciones
Corrugator (1) ──── consume ──── (N) Reel [vía RollStand] Corrugator (1) ───- ejecuta ──── (1) ProductionOrder Corrugator (1) ──── usa ──── (1-N) PaperGrade Corrugator (1) ──── genera ──── (N) Failure Corrugator (1) ──── mide ──── (1) KPIEngine Corrugator (1) ──── registra_costes ──── (1) FinancialEngine Corrugator (1) ───- alimentado_por ──── (5) RollStand


---

## Lifecycle
1. **Inicialización**: speed=0, status=IDLE
2. **Warm-up** (1 turno): producción normal pero no contabilizada
3. **Operación**: ciclos de SETUP → RUNNING → CHANGING → RUNNING
4. **Mantenimiento**: cada 720h (30 días) inspección completa
5. **Overhaul**: anual (8.760h)
6. **Cierre**: snapshot final con totales

---

## Algoritmos de cálculo

### Cálculo de OEE (cada 60s)
Availability (A) = (PlannedTime - DownTime) / PlannedTime Performance (P) = (ActualSpeed / TheoreticalSpeed) × Availability_Factor Quality (Q) = GoodUnits / TotalUnits OEE = A × P × Q × 100


### Cálculo de producción
production_m = current_speed × tick_duration_s / 60 waste_m = production_m × waste_rate_pct good_production_m = production_m - waste_m


### Cálculo de consumo de papel
paper_consumed_kg = good_production_m × paper_gramage × paper_width / 1e6


---

## Parámetros de Configuración

```yaml
# config_corrugator.yaml
corrugator:
  name: "Corrugator Configuration"
  category: "production_equipment"
  
  speed:
    max_speed_m_min: 350
    average_speed_m_min: 220
    min_speed_m_min: 50
    speed_variability_pct: 8  # ±8% de variación natural
    
  dimensions:
    paper_width_mm: 2500
    max_paper_width_mm: 2800
    
  production:
    waste_rate_pct: 1.0  # % de desperdicio
    quality_threshold_pct: 99.0
    
  reliability:
    mtbf_h: 200  # Mean Time Between Failures
    mttr_min: 45  # Mean Time To Repair
    failure_distribution: "weibull"
    failure_types:
      - type: "belt_tear"
        probability: 0.25
        mttr_mean: 30
      - type: "glue_unit_failure"
        probability: 0.20
        mttr_mean: 60
      - type: "heater_failure"
        probability: 0.15
        mttr_mean: 90
      - type: "cutting_unit"
        probability: 0.15
        mttr_mean: 45
      - type: "electrical"
        probability: 0.15
        mttr_mean: 30
      - type: "sensor_fault"
        probability: 0.10
        mttr_mean: 20
        
  maintenance:
    pm_interval_h: 720  # Preventivo cada 30 días
    pm_duration_h: 8
    cleaning_interval_h: 16  # Cada 16h operativas
    cleaning_duration_min: 30
    overhaul_interval_h: 8760  # Anual
    overhaul_duration_h: 72
    
  setup:
    avg_setup_time_min: 20
    setup_time_std_min: 5
    
  oee:
    target_pct: 85
    min_acceptable_pct: 75
    
  validation:
    cross_parameter_rules:
      - rule: "min_speed < average_speed < max_speed"
      - rule: "mtbf > 0 AND mttr > 0"
      - rule: "sum(failure_types.probability) == 1.0"
      - rule: "quality_threshold > 95"
      
  kpi_impacted:
    - "OEE_pct"
    - "availability_pct"
    - "performance_pct"
    - "quality_pct"
    - "production_m_per_h"
    - "production_m_per_turno"
    - "production_m_per_year"
    - "starvation_events_per_turno"
    - "lost_minutes_per_turno"
    - "downtime_pct"
    - "failures_per_month"
    - "LPI"
    - "annual_savings_eur"
    
  risk: "crítico"
  priority: "crítica"
Reglas de Validación
R1: min_speed < average_speed < max_speed
R2: 0 ≤ current_speed ≤ max_speed
R3: OEE = Availability × Performance × Quality (en todo momento)
R4: production_good + production_waste = total_production
R5: Si speed < avg * 0.8 por > 30s → estado SLOWDOWN
R6: Si status == STARVED por > 30s → evento de starvation
R7: sum(failure_types.probability) == 1.0
KPIs generados
KPI	Fórmula	Frecuencia
OEE %	A × P × Q	Cada 60s
Availability %	(Planned - Down) / Planned	Cada 60s
Performance %	ActualSpeed / TheoreticalSpeed	Cada 60s
Quality %	Good / Total	Cada 60s
Production m/h	sum(production) / hours	Continuo
Production m/turno	sum(production) / shifts	Por turno
Production m/año	sum(production) / 330 days	Anual
Downtime %	DownTime / PlannedTime	Por turno
Starvation Events	count(STARVED > 30s)	Por turno
Paper Consumed kg/h	production × gramage × width	Continuo
Algoritmos relacionados
algo_13_oee_calculation.md → cálculo OEE
algo_10_failure_generation.md → generación de fallos
algo_09_starvation_prediction.md → predicción de starvation
Riesgos específicos
Riesgo	Probabilidad	Impacto	Mitigación
Fallo catastrófico	Baja (0.3%)	Crítico	MTBF 200h, MTTR 45min
Starvation prolongada	Media	Crítico	Buffer staging + predicción
Calidad < 99%	Media	Alto	SPC + alertas tempranas
Cambio lento	Media	Medio	avg_change_time=45s
Mantenimiento no programado	Media	Alto	PM cada 720h
Prioridad de desarrollo
Crítica — Es el activo más valioso de la planta.


---

# 📄 ARCHIVO 2: `02_SIMULATION_MODEL/07_Forklift.md`

```markdown
# 07 – Forklift
# INGETRANS Reel Loading Simulator V4

## Propósito
Recurso móvil (carretilla elevadora) que transporta reels entre el warehouse, el exchange zone, los tracks y los roll stands. Es el método de logística **convencional** (Scenario A baseline).

## Entradas
- Tareas de dispatching desde Logistics Engine
- Reels disponibles en warehouse
- Demandas de los roll stands (carga/retorno)
- Estado de la batería/combustible

## Salidas
- Reel recogido del warehouse (PICKUP)
- Reel entregado al exchange/track (DROPOFF)
- Reel retornado al warehouse (RETURN)
- Eventos de fallo y mantenimiento
- Distancia recorrida (KPI)

## Configuración
Ver `03_CONFIG_DATABASE/config_forklift.yaml`

## Dependencias
- Depende de: Operator, Warehouse, Exchange, Track, RollStand
- Consumida por: Logistics Engine, KPI Engine, Financial Engine, Animation Engine

## Validación
- position válida en planta
- max 1 reel simultáneo
- battery ≥ 0
- payload ≤ max_load

## KPIs afectados
- **Forklift Utilization**
- **Forklift Travel Distance (km/año)**
- **Average Delivery Time**
- **Average Response Time**
- **Average Waiting Time**
- **Reel Deliveries/h**
- **Reel Returns/h**
- **LPI**

## Riesgo
- **Alto**: forklift único = single point of failure

## Prioridad
- **Crítica**

---

## Atributos

| Atributo | Tipo | Unidad | Default | Min | Max | Obligatorio |
|---|---|---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| forklift_id | str | - | "FL-01" | - | - | Sí |
| operator_id | str | - | "OP-01" | - | - | Sí |
| status | str | - | "idle" | - | - | Sí |
| position_x | float | m | 0.0 | - | - | Sí |
| position_y | float | m | 0.0 | - | - | Sí |
| speed_loaded | float | m/min | 60 | 20 | 120 | Sí |
| speed_empty | float | m/min | 80 | 30 | 150 | Sí |
| max_load_kg | float | kg | 4000 | 2000 | 8000 | Sí |
| current_payload | Reel | - | null | - | - | No |
| battery_pct | float | % | 100 | 0 | 100 | Sí |
| fuel_pct | float | % | 100 | 0 | 100 | Sí |
| odometer_km | float | km | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| hours_worked | float | h | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| last_maintenance_h | float | h | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| mtbf_h | float | h | 80 | 20 | 500 | Sí |
| mttr_min | float | min | 30 | 5 | 240 | Sí |
| current_task | Task | - | null | - | - | No |
| task_queue | list | - | [] | - | - | Sí |
| num_tasks_completed | int | Nº | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |

---

## Estados (State Machine)

IDLE → DISPATCHED → TRAVELING_LOADED → PICKING_UP → TRAVELING_LOADED → DROPPING_OFF → TRAVELING_EMPTY → IDLE ↘ FAILURE → MAINTENANCE → IDLE ↘ BREAK → IDLE ↘ SHIFT_END → IDLE ↘ BATTERY_LOW → CHARGING → IDLE


### Transiciones
| Desde | Evento | Hacia | Condición |
|---|---|---|---|
| IDLE | task_assigned | DISPATCHED | - |
| DISPATCHED | travel_start | TRAVELING_LOADED o TRAVELING_EMPTY | - |
| TRAVELING_EMPTY | arrived | PICKING_UP | - |
| PICKING_UP | pickup_complete | TRAVELING_LOADED | - |
| TRAVELING_LOADED | arrived | DROPPING_OFF | - |
| DROPPING_OFF | dropoff_complete | TRAVELING_EMPTY | - |
| TRAVELING_EMPTY | returned | IDLE | - |
| * | random_check | FAILURE | random() < failure_prob |
| FAILURE | repair_complete | IDLE | - |
| * | break_window | BREAK | - |
| BREAK | break_complete | IDLE | - |
| * | shift_end | SHIFT_END | - |
| SHIFT_END | shift_start | IDLE | - |
| * | battery_low | CHARGING | battery < 20% |
| CHARGING | charged | IDLE | battery >= 95% |

---

## Inputs
1. Task de dispatching (Logistics Engine)
2. Posición del warehouse/exchange/track destino
3. Evento de fallo (Failure Engine)
4. Señal de break/fin de turno (Calendar)
5. Battery level updates (Energy Manager)

## Outputs
1. **Posición actualizada** (cada tick, 1s)
2. **Eventos**: FORKLIFT_DISPATCHED, FORKLIFT_PICKUP, FORKLIFT_DROPOFF, FORKLIFT_RETURN, FORKLIFT_FAILURE
3. **KPI live**: utilization, distance traveled, tasks completed
4. **Estado batería/combustible**
5. **Alertas**: BATTERY_LOW, MAINTENANCE_DUE, FAILURE

---

## Relaciones
Forklift (1) ───- operado_por ──── (1) Operator Forklift (1) ──── recoge_de ──── (1) Warehouse Forklift (1) ──── entrega_a ──── (1) Exchange Forklift (1) ──── entrega_a ──── (N) Track Forklift (1) ───- retorna_a ──── (1) Warehouse Forklift (1) ──── mide ──── (1) KPIEngine Forklift (1) ──── genera ──── (N) Failure Forklift (1) ──── consume ──── (1) Energy


---

## Lifecycle
1. **Inicialización**: position en warehouse, battery=100%, status=IDLE
2. **Operación**: ciclo dispatch → travel → pickup → travel → dropoff → return
3. **Carga/Combustible**: cada X km o cambio de turno
4. **Mantenimiento**: cada 250h o por evento
5. **Reemplazo**: tras 15,000h o avería mayor

---

## Algoritmos de comportamiento

### Cálculo de tiempo de viaje
```python
distance_m = euclidean_distance(current_pos, target_pos)
travel_time_s = (distance_m / current_speed) * 60 + acceleration_overhead
Dispatching rules (seleccionables)
FIFO: primera tarea asignada primero
NEAREST_IDLE: forklift más cercano al pickup point
PRIORITY_BASED: tareas urgentes primero
ROUND_ROBIN: rotación entre roll stands
EDD: Earliest Due Date
Búsqueda de path
def find_path(start, end):
    if congestion_avoidance:
        return shortest_path_avoiding_congestion(start, end)
    else:
        return shortest_path(start, end)
Parámetros de Configuración
# config_forklift.yaml (resumen - el completo ya está generado)
forklift:
  name: "Forklift FL-01"
  category: "mobile_equipment"
  scenario: "A_baseline"
  
  kinematics:
    speed_loaded_m_min: 60
    speed_empty_m_min: 80
    acceleration_m_s2: 0.8
    deceleration_m_s2: 1.0
    turning_radius_m: 2.5
    max_load_kg: 4000
    
  service_times:
    pickup_time_s: 30
    dropoff_time_s: 20
    search_time_s: 25
    waiting_time_s: 20
    maneuver_time_s: 15
    
  shift_breaks:
    shift_change_delay_min: 5
    break_duration_min: 15
    break_frequency: 2
    
  reliability:
    availability_pct: 92
    mtbf_h: 80
    mttr_min: 30
    failure_distribution: "exponential"
    
  energy:
    type: "electric"
    battery_capacity_kwh: 80
    consumption_kwh_per_km: 1.2
    charging_time_h: 4
    
  routing:
    dispatching_rule: "nearest_idle"
    path_planning: "shortest_path"
    collision_avoidance: true
    congestion_threshold_pct: 75
    
  risks:
    - "single_point_of_failure_if_num=1"
    - "operator_dependent_speed"
    - "battery_limited_range"
Reglas de Validación
R1: current_payload == null XOR (status in [PICKING_UP, TRAVELING_LOADED, DROPPING_OFF])
R2: battery_pct ≥ 0 AND ≤ 100
R3: max_load ≥ max_reel_weight × 1.1
R4: Si status == FAILURE → no aceptar nuevas tareas
R5: task_queue.length ≤ max_queue_size (default 10)
R6: odometer_km monotonically increasing
KPIs generados
KPI	Fórmula	Frecuencia
Forklift Utilization %	busy_time / available_time	Continuo
Travel Distance km	sum(travel_segments)	Continuo
Travel Distance km/año	sum / 330 days	Anual
Tasks Completed	count(completed_tasks)	Continuo
Avg Delivery Time	mean(delivery_durations)	Continuo
Avg Response Time	mean(response_durations)	Continuo
Battery Cycles	count(charge_cycles)	Diario
Failures/mes	count(failures) / month	Mensual
Maintenance Events	count(maintenance)	Mensual
Algoritmos relacionados
algo_06_forklift_dispatching.md → reglas de dispatching
algo_03_warehouse_selection.md → selección origen
algo_04_track_assignment.md → selección destino
algo_10_failure_generation.md → generación de fallos
Riesgos específicos
Riesgo	Probabilidad	Impacto	Mitigación
Fallo en operación	Media (8%/mes)	Alto	MTBF 80h, MTTR 30min
Operador ausente	Baja (1%)	Alto	Backup operator protocol
Batería agotada	Baja	Alto	Charging opportunístico
Colisión con transfer	Baja	Medio	Collision avoidance
Cambio de bobina erróneo	Baja (0.5%)	Medio	Scanner verification
Bobina dañada	Baja (0.2%)	Bajo	Manejo cuidadoso + velocidad limitada
Comparativa Forklift vs INGETRANS
Aspecto	Forklift	INGETRANS
Velocidad carga	60 m/min	80 m/min
Tiempo pickup	30 s	6 s
Tiempo dropoff	20 s	6 s
Tiempo búsqueda	25 s	0 s
Operador requerido	Sí	No
Errores	0.5%	0%
Disponibilidad	92%	97%
Coste operativo	35 €/h	4 €/h (mantto)
Coste anual	~250 k€	~4 k€ + CAPEX
Prioridad de desarrollo
Crítica — Es el principal recurso logístico del Scenario A.

# 📄 ARCHIVO 3: `02_SIMULATION_MODEL/08_AutomaticTransfer.md`

```markdown
# 08 – Automatic Transfer (INGETRANS)
# INGETRANS Reel Loading Simulator V4

## Propósito
Recurso activo automático que circula por el transfer track, recoge reels del warehouse y los entrega a los roll stands. Es el método de logística **automática INGETRANS** (Scenario B). No requiere operador humano, tiene mayor velocidad de pickup/dropoff y menor tasa de errores.

## Entradas
- Demandas de los roll stands (vía Logistics Engine)
- Reels disponibles en warehouse
- Posición de los stops del transfer track
- Estado de mantenimiento

## Salidas
- Reel recogido del warehouse (PICKUP)
- Reel entregado al roll stand (DROPOFF)
- Reel retornado al warehouse (RETURN)
- Eventos de cycle start/end
- Posición y velocidad actuales

## Configuración
Ver `03_CONFIG_DATABASE/config_ingetrans.yaml`

## Dependencias
- Depende de: Transfer (infraestructura), Warehouse, RollStand
- Consumida por: Logistics Engine, KPI Engine, Financial Engine, Animation Engine

## Validación
- position en stops válidos
- max 2 reels simultáneos
- speed ∈ [0, max_speed]
- cycle_time computable

## KPIs afectados
- **Transfer Utilization**
- **Transfer Cycle Time**
- **Average Delivery Time** (52 s vs 115 s forklift)
- **Average Response Time** (15 s vs 42 s forklift)
- **Reel Deliveries/h**
- **LPI**
- **Annual Savings** (€260-340k)

## Riesgo
- **Medio**: alta confiabilidad, pero fallo = parada automática

## Prioridad
- **Crítica**

---

## Atributos

| Atributo | Tipo | Unidad | Default | Min | Max | Obligatorio |
|---|---|---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| transfer_id | str | - | "AT-01" | - | - | Sí |
| status | str | - | "idle" | - | - | Sí |
| position_x | float | m | 0.0 | - | - | Sí |
| position_y | float | m | 2.5 | - | - | Sí |
| current_speed | float | m/min | 0 | 0 | 80 | Sí |
| max_speed | float | m/min | 80 | 50 | 120 | Sí |
| acceleration_ramp_s | float | s | 4.5 | 2.0 | 10.0 | Sí |
| deceleration_ramp_s | float | s | 4.5 | 2.0 | 10.0 | Sí |
| start_stop_overhead_s | float | s | 9.0 | 5.0 | 15.0 | Sí |
| pickup_time_s | float | s | 6.0 | 3.0 | 15.0 | Sí |
| dropoff_time_s | float | s | 6.0 | 3.0 | 15.0 | Sí |
| capacity_reels | int | reels | 2 | 1 | 4 | Sí |
| current_payload | list(Reel) | - | [] | - | - | Sí |
| current_stop | str | - | "S-00" | - | - | Sí |
| target_stop | str | - | null | - | - | No |
| num_cycles_completed | int | Nº | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| total_distance_m | float | m | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| total_operating_h | float | h | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| mtbf_h | float | h | 500 | 100 | 2000 | Sí |
| mttr_min | float | min | 60 | 15 | 480 | Sí |

---

## Estados (State Machine)

IDLE → ACCELERATING → CRUISING → DECELERATING → PICKING_UP → RETURNING → DROPPING_OFF → IDLE ↘ FAILURE → MAINTENANCE → IDLE ↘ EMERGENCY_STOP → IDLE


### Transiciones
| Desde | Evento | Hacia | Condición |
|---|---|---|---|
| IDLE | cycle_start | ACCELERATING | target_stop definido |
| ACCELERATING | ramp_complete | CRUISING | elapsed ≥ 4.5s |
| CRUISING | arrived_target | DECELERATING | position == target |
| DECELERATING | ramp_complete | PICKING_UP o DROPPING_OFF | elapsed ≥ 4.5s |
| PICKING_UP | pickup_complete | RETURNING o CRUISING | - |
| DROPPING_OFF | dropoff_complete | RETURNING o CRUISING | - |
| RETURNING | arrived_warehouse | IDLE | - |
| * | failure_detected | FAILURE | random() < failure_prob |
| FAILURE | repair_complete | IDLE | - |
| * | emergency_signal | EMERGENCY_STOP | - |
| EMERGENCY_STOP | reset_complete | IDLE | manual reset |

---

## Inputs
1. Demanda de reel desde RollStand (vía Logistics Engine)
2. Posición actual de stops
3. Estado del track (blocked/unblocked)
4. Evento de fallo
5. Comando de emergencia (safety system)

## Outputs
1. **Posición + velocidad** (cada tick, 1s)
2. **Eventos**: TRANSFER_CYCLE_START, TRANSFER_PICKUP, TRANSFER_DROPOFF, TRANSFER_RETURN
3. **KPI live**: utilization, cycle time, num cycles
4. **Estado operacional**
5. **Alertas**: FAILURE, EMERGENCY_STOP, MAINTENANCE_DUE

---

## Relaciones
AutomaticTransfer (1) ───- se_mueve_en ──── (1) Transfer [infraestructura] AutomaticTransfer (1) ──── recoge_de ──── (1) Warehouse AutomaticTransfer (1) ───- entrega_a ──── (N) RollStand AutomaticTransfer (1) ───- retorna_a ──── (1) Warehouse AutomaticTransfer (1) ──── mide ──── (1) KPIEngine AutomaticTransfer (1) ──── genera ──── (N) Failure


---

## Lifecycle
1. **Inicialización**: position=S-00 (warehouse), status=IDLE
2. **Operación**: ciclo continuo warehouse → stand → stand → ... → warehouse
3. **Mantenimiento**: cada 720h inspección
4. **Overhaul**: cada 8.760h (anual)
5. **Cierre**: snapshot final con totales

---

## Algoritmos de comportamiento

### Cálculo de tiempo de ciclo completo
```python
def calculate_cycle_time(distance_to_stand, distance_return):
    # Aceleración + Crucero + Desaceleración
    accel_time = acceleration_ramp_s  # 4.5s
    decel_time = deceleration_ramp_s  # 4.5s
    
    # Distancia durante ramps (trapezoidal)
    accel_distance = (max_speed/2) * (accel_time/60)  # m
    decel_distance = (max_speed/2) * (decel_time/60)  # m
    
    # Crucero
    cruise_distance = max(0, distance_to_stand - accel_distance - decel_distance)
    cruise_time = (cruise_distance / max_speed) * 60  # s
    
    # Tiempo total de un viaje
    travel_time = accel_time + cruise_time + decel_time + start_stop_overhead
    
    # Tiempo de servicio
    service_time = pickup_time + dropoff_time  # 12s total
    
    # Ciclo completo (ida + vuelta con pickup/dropoff)
    cycle_time = (travel_time * 2) + service_time + 10  # +10s buffer warehouse
    return cycle_time
Ejemplo numérico (50 m de distancia):

Aceleración: 4.5s
Crucero: (50 - 2.7 - 2.7) / 80 × 60 = 33.5s
Desaceleración: 4.5s
Overhead: 9s
Pickup + dropoff: 12s
Total: ~64s (vs ~150s forklift para misma distancia)
Parámetros de Configuración
# config_ingetrans.yaml
automatic_transfer:
  name: "INGETRANS Automatic Transfer"
  category: "automatic_equipment"
  scenario: "B_ingetrans"
  
  kinematics:
    max_speed_m_min: 80
    acceleration_ramp_s: 4.5
    deceleration_ramp_s: 4.5
    start_stop_overhead_s: 9
    positioning_accuracy_mm: 50
    
  service_times:
    pickup_time_s: 6
    dropoff_time_s: 6
    pre_pickup_positioning_s: 2
    post_dropoff_verification_s: 2
    
  capacity:
    max_reels: 2
    min_reels: 1
    delivery_strategy: "single"  # single | batch
    
  scheduling:
    strategy: "next_demand_edd"  # nearest | edd | priority
    allow_batch: true
    max_batch_size: 2
    
  reliability:
    availability_pct: 97
    mtbf_h: 500
    mttr_min: 60
    failure_distribution: "weibull"
    failure_types:
      - type: "servo_motor"
        probability: 0.30
        mttr_mean: 90
      - type: "encoder_fault"
        probability: 0.20
        mttr_mean: 30
      - type: "gripper_failure"
        probability: 0.20
        mttr_mean: 45
      - type: "rail_alignment"
        probability: 0.15
        mttr_mean: 120
      - type: "electrical"
        probability: 0.15
        mttr_mean: 30

    - "reel_deliveries_per_h"
    - "LPI"
    - "annual_savings_eur"
    - "payback_years"
    - "ROI_pct"
    
  risk: "medio"
  priority: "crítica"
Reglas de Validación

R2: 0 ≤ current_speed ≤ max_speed

R4: cycle_time computable en < 200s
R5: Si status == FAILURE → no aceptar nuevas tareas
R6: pickup_time + dropoff_time < 30s (ventaja competitiva)
KPIs generados

# 📄 ARCHIVO 4: `02_SIMULATION_MODEL/09_Operator.md`

# 09 – Operator
# INGETRANS Reel Loading Simulator V4

## Propósito
Recurso humano que opera el forklift (Scenario A). Controla velocidad, ejecuta pickups/dropoffs, gestiona prioridades de tareas y reacciona a eventos inesperados. En el Scenario B (INGETRANS) no se requiere operador para el transfer automático.

## Entradas
- Turnos de trabajo (Shift Calendar)
- Tareas asignadas al forklift
- Eventos de break, ausencia, fin de turno
- Estado del forklift (fallos, batería)

## Salidas
- Acciones ejecutadas en el forklift
- Eventos OPERATOR_ABSENT, BREAK_START, SHIFT_END
- Productividad (reels/h manipulados)
- Coste laboral (€/h)

## Configuración
Ver `03_CONFIG_DATABASE/config_operator.yaml`

## Dependencias
- Depende de: Forklift, Shift, Calendar
- Consumida por: Forklift (asignación), KPI Engine, Financial Engine

## Validación
- 1 operador ↔ 1 forklift (1:1)
- presencia ∈ {true, false}
- turno actual ∈ turnos definidos

## KPIs afectados
- Forklift Utilization (indirectamente)
- Labor Cost (€/h)
- Productivity (reels/h)
- Absenteeism Rate
- LPI (componente 0.10)

## Riesgo
- **Medio**: ausencia no programada = parada forklift

## Prioridad
- **Alta**

---

## Atributos

| Atributo | Tipo | Unidad | Default | Min | Max | Obligatorio |
|---|---|---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| operator_id | str | - | "OP-01" | - | - | Sí |
| name | str | - | "John Doe" | - | - | Sí |
| forklift_id | str | - | "FL-01" | - | - | Sí |
| status | str | - | "on_shift" | - | - | Sí |
| shift_id | str | - | "S-DAY" | - | - | Sí |
| skill_level | int | 1-5 | 3 | 1 | 5 | Sí |
| certification_date | date | - | - | - | - | No |
| absence_probability_pct | float | % | 1.0 | 0 | 10 | Sí |
| cost_per_hour_eur | float | €/h | 35 | 15 | 80 | Sí |
| hours_worked_today | float | h | 0 | 0 | 12 | Sí |
| breaks_taken_today | int | Nº | 0 | 0 | 5 | Sí |
| productivity_score | float | 1.0 | 1.0 | 0.5 | 1.5 | Sí |
| error_rate_multiplier | float | 1.0 | 1.0 | 0.5 | 2.0 | Sí |

---

## Estados (State Machine)

OFF_SHIFT → ON_SHIFT → ACTIVE → BREAK → ACTIVE ↓ ABSENT → OFF_SHIFT ↓ TRAINING → ON_SHIFT


### Transiciones
| Desde | Evento | Hacia | Condición |
|---|---|---|---|
| OFF_SHIFT | shift_start | ON_SHIFT | tiempo == shift.inicio |
| ON_SHIFT | handover_complete | ACTIVE | - |
| ACTIVE | break_window | BREAK | elapsed >= break_time |
| BREAK | break_complete | ACTIVE | elapsed >= break_duration |
| ACTIVE | random_check | ABSENT | random() < absence_prob |
| ABSENT | shift_end | OFF_SHIFT | - |
| ABSENT | replacement_arrives | ACTIVE | - |
| * | training_scheduled | TRAINING | - |
| TRAINING | training_complete | ON_SHIFT | - |

---

## Inputs
1. Shift calendar (horarios)
2. Tareas del forklift
3. Eventos de break programado
4. Evento aleatorio de ausencia
5. Evento de training/capacitación

## Outputs
1. Acciones en forklift (velocidad, ruta, prioridad)
2. Eventos: OPERATOR_PRESENT, OPERATOR_ABSENT, BREAK_START, SHIFT_START
3. Métricas de productividad
4. Coste laboral acumulado

## Relaciones

---

## Lifecycle
1. **Contratación**: skill_level asignado, certification
2. **Operación diaria**: shift → active → breaks → shift end
3. **Capacitación**: training periódico
4. **Ausencias**: eventos aleatorios o planificados
5. **Renuncia/despido**: replacement operator

## Algoritmos de comportamiento

### Efecto del skill_level en performance
```python
def get_speed_multiplier(skill_level):
    # skill 1 (novato): 0.85x speed
    # skill 3 (medio): 1.00x speed
    # skill 5 (experto): 1.15x speed
    return 0.85 + (skill_level - 1) * 0.075

def get_error_multiplier(skill_level):
    # skill 1: 1.5x errors
    # skill 3: 1.0x errors
    # skill 5: 0.5x errors
    return 1.75 - (skill_level - 1) * 0.25
Cálculo de productividad diaria
productivity = (
    (hours_worked - breaks_duration) 
    * skill_multiplier 
    * health_factor
)
Parámetros de Configuración
# config_operator.yaml
operator:
  name: "Operator Configuration"
  category: "human_resource"
  
  workforce:
    num_operators: 1
    rotation: "fixed_forklift"  # operador siempre al mismo forklift
    backup_operator: false
    
  shifts:
    - shift_id: "S-DAY"
      start_time: "06:00"
      end_time: "14:00"
      operator_ids: ["OP-01"]
    - shift_id: "S-NIGHT"
      start_time: "14:00"
      end_time: "22:00"
      operator_ids: ["OP-02"]
      
  breaks:
    break_times: ["10:00", "12:00"]  # en horario 06:00-14:00
    break_duration_min: 15
    break_frequency_per_shift: 2
    
  absence:
    probability_pct: 1.0
    unplanned_absence: true
    planned_absence_days: ["2024-08-15", "2024-12-25"]
    replacement_protocol: "call_backup_or_halt"
    
  skills:
    skill_levels: [3, 4, 3, 5, 2]  # 5 operadores
    certifications_required:
      - "forklift_license"
      - "safety_training"
      - "paper_handling"
      
  costs:
    cost_per_hour_eur: 35
    overtime_multiplier: 1.5
    night_shift_multiplier: 1.25
    weekend_multiplier: 1.35
    benefits_pct: 30  # % sobre salary
    
  productivity:
    base_productivity: 1.0
    fatigue_factor_per_hour: 0.02  # -2% por hora trabajada
    motivation_random_events: true
    
  validation:
    cross_parameter_rules:
      - rule: "num_operators >= num_forklifts"
      - rule: "cost_per_hour > 0"
      - rule: "break_duration > 0"
      - rule: "absence_probability <= 10"
      
  kpi_impacted:
    - "forklift_utilization_pct"
    - "labor_cost_eur_per_year"
    - "productivity_reels_per_h"
    - "absenteeism_rate_pct"
    - "wrong_reel_events_count"
    - "LPI"
    
  risk: "medio"
  priority: "alta"
Reglas de Validación
R1: 1 operador ↔ max 1 forklift simultáneamente
R2: operator.forklift_id == forklift.operator_id (consistencia)
R3: presence == true mientras status == ACTIVE
R4: hours_worked_today ≤ 12h (límite legal)
R5: breaks_taken_today == break_frequency al final del turno
KPIs generados
KPI	Fórmula	Frecuencia
Productivity (reels/h)	count_reels / hours_active	Diario
Labor Cost (€/year)	sum(hours * cost)	Anual
Absenteeism Rate %	count_absences / total_shifts	Mensual
Avg Skill Level	mean(skill_levels)	-
Training Hours/year	sum(training_time)	Anual
Algoritmos relacionados
algo_06_forklift_dispatching.md → productividad del operador
algo_12_recovery.md → recovery de ausencias
Riesgos específicos
Riesgo	Probabilidad	Impacto	Mitigación
Ausencia no planificada	Media (1%)	Alto	Backup operator protocol
Error humano	Media (0.5%)	Medio	Training + verificación
Fatiga	Baja	Medio	Límite 12h + breaks
Accidente	Muy baja	Crítico	Safety training
Baja definitiva	Baja	Alto	Pool de replacements
Comparativa con INGETRANS (sin operador)
Aspecto	Con Operador	Sin Operador (INGETRANS)
Coste horario	35 €/h	0 €/h
Coste anual	246,400 € (2 shifts)	0 €
Errores por turno	0.5% × 44 = 0.22	0
Velocidad	Variable (skill)	Constante
Disponibilidad	99% (con backup)	97% (sin backup humano)
Fatiga	Sí	No
Ausencias	Posibles	Imposibles
Training	Requerido	No requerido
Prioridad de desarrollo

# 📄 ARCHIVO 5: `02_SIMULATION_MODEL/10_Reel.md`

```markdown
# 10 – Reel
# INGETRANS Reel Loading Simulator V4

## Propósito
Entidad fluida que representa una bobina de papel individual. Es la unidad mínima de transporte y consumo. Tiene identidad propia (RFID/QR), atributos físicos (diámetro, peso, ancho, gramaje) y un ciclo de vida completo desde creación hasta consumo o descarte.

## Entradas
- Producción externa (replenishment del warehouse)
- Retorno desde tracks (reel usado con remaining %)
- Demandas desde corrugadora (paper grade específico)
- Eventos de daño o error

## Salidas
- Consumo de metros lineales (a corrugadora)
- Remaining % al retorno
- Peso y dimensiones físicas
- Eventos: REEL_CREATED, REEL_CONSUMED, REEL_RETURNED, REEL_DAMAGED, REEL_WRONG

## Configuración
Ver `03_CONFIG_DATABASE/config_reel.yaml`

## Dependencias
- Depende de: PaperGrade, Warehouse, Track, RollStand, Corrugator
- Consumida por: TODAS las entidades (es la entidad núcleo)

## Validación
- diameter ∈ [min, max]
- weight ∈ [min, max]
- width ∈ [min, max]
- remaining ∈ [0, 100]
- status transiciones válidas

## KPIs afectados
- Reel Changes/h
- Reel Deliveries/h
- Reel Returns/h
- Remaining % at Return
- Paper Consumption (kg)
- Quality Rate (good reels / total reels)

## Riesgo
- **Bajo**: entidad pasiva, solo es trackeada

## Prioridad
- **Crítica** — Es la entidad central del flujo

---

## Atributos

| Atributo | Tipo | Unidad | Default | Min | Max | Obligatorio |
|---|---|---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| reel_id | str | - | "R-XXXXX" | - | - | Sí |
| paper_grade_id | str | - | "PG-01" | - | - | Sí |
| diameter_initial_mm | float | mm | 1500 | 850 | 1500 | Sí |
| diameter_current_mm | float | mm | 1500 | 0 | 1500 | Sí |
| width_mm | float | mm | 2500 | 1800 | 3500 | Sí |
| weight_initial_kg | float | kg | 2100 | 800 | 3500 | Sí |
| weight_current_kg | float | kg | 2100 | 0 | 3500 | Sí |
| length_initial_m | float | m | 12000 | 5000 | 25000 | Sí |
| length_consumed_m | float | m | 0 | 0 | length_initial | Sí |
| length_remaining_m | float | m | 12000 | 0 | 12000 | Sí |
| remaining_pct | float | % | 100 | 0 | 100 | Sí |
| status | str | - | "in_warehouse" | - | - | Sí |
| location | str | - | "WH-01" | - | - | Sí |
| creation_ts | timestamp | s | 0 | - | - | Sí |
| last_update_ts | timestamp | s | 0 | - | - | Sí |
| rfid_code | str | - | "RFID-XXX" | - | - | Sí |
| batch_id | str | - | "B-XXXX" | - | - | No |
| supplier_id | str | - | "SUP-01" | - | - | No |
| quality_grade | str | - | "A" | - | - | No |
| damage_marks | list | - | [] | - | - | No |
| cost_eur | float | € | 1200 | 800 | 2000 | Sí |

---

## Estados (State Machine)

IN_WAREHOUSE → ALLOCATED → IN_TRANSIT → AT_EXCHANGE → ON_TRACK → IN_USE → RETURN_REQUESTED → IN_RETURN → IN_WAREHOUSE ↘ WRONG_REEL → SCRAPPED ↘ DAMAGED → SCRAPPED ↘ CONSUMED → END


### Transiciones
| Desde | Evento | Hacia | Condición |
|---|---|---|---|
| IN_WAREHOUSE | allocated | ALLOCATED | paper_grade demandada |
| ALLOCATED | dispatched | IN_TRANSIT | forklift/transfer recoge |
| IN_TRANSIT | arrived_exchange | AT_EXCHANGE | - |
| AT_EXCHANGE | delivered_track | ON_TRACK | - |
| ON_TRACK | loaded_stand | IN_USE | - |
| IN_USE | reel_finished | RETURN_REQUESTED | remaining < threshold |
| RETURN_REQUESTED | removed_track | IN_RETURN | - |
| IN_RETURN | arrived_warehouse | IN_WAREHOUSE | - |
| * | wrong_grade_detected | WRONG_REEL | - |
| * | damage_detected | DAMAGED | - |
| WRONG_REEL o DAMAGED | scrapped | SCRAPPED | - |
| IN_USE | fully_consumed | CONSUMED | remaining == 0 |

---

## Inputs
1. **Replenishment order** → REEL_CREATED
2. **Allocation request** desde Logistics Engine → REEL_ALLOCATED
3. **Consumo en corrugadora** → REEL_CONSUMED (parcial)
4. **Retorno desde track** → REEL_RETURNED
5. **Daño físico** → REEL_DAMAGED
6. **Error de paper grade** → REEL_WRONG

## Outputs
1. **Posición actual** (warehouse/exchange/track/stand)
2. **Remaining %** (live)
3. **Eventos**: REEL_CREATED, REEL_ALLOCATED, REEL_IN_TRANSIT, REEL_LOADED, REEL_CHANGED, REEL_CONSUMED, REEL_RETURNED, REEL_DAMAGED
4. **Consumo de papel** (kg, m)
5. **Métricas de calidad** (1 si good, 0 si damaged)

---

## Relaciones
Reel (N) ──── pertenece_a ──── (1) PaperGrade Reel (1) ──── almacenado_en ──── (1) Warehouse Reel (1) ───- transportado_por ──── (1) Forklift | AutomaticTransfer Reel (1) ──── ubicado_en ──── (1) Exchange | Track | RollStand Reel (1) ───- consumido_por ──── (1) Corrugator Reel (1) ──── medido_por ──── (1) KPIEngine Reel (1) ──── genera ──── (N) Event


---

## Lifecycle detallado

### Fase 1: Creación
- Recibido del proveedor
- Inspección de calidad
- Asignación de RFID
- Almacenado en warehouse (slot asignado por paper grade)

### Fase 2: Asignación
- Logística selecciona reel según paper grade demandada
- Verificación RFID
- Asignación a tarea de transporte

### Fase 3: Transporte
- Pickup del warehouse
- Viaje a exchange zone
- Entrega al track

### Fase 4: Espera
- En track (waiting para uso)
- O en staging buffer

### Fase 5: Consumo
- Cargado en roll stand
- Corrugadora consume metros
- Remaining % decrece

### Fase 6: Retorno (si remaining > 0)
- Retirado del stand
- Retornado al warehouse
- Reutilizado si remaining > threshold

### Fase 7: Disposición final
- Si remaining == 0 → CONSUMED → END
- Si DAMAGED → SCRAPPED → END
- Si WRONG_REEL → SCRAPPED → END

---

## Algoritmos de cálculo

### Cálculo de remaining % durante consumo
```python
def update_remaining(reel, meters_consumed):
    reel.length_consumed_m += meters_consumed
    reel.length_remaining_m -= meters_consumed
    reel.remaining_pct = (reel.length_remaining_m / reel.length_initial_m) * 100
    reel.diameter_current_mm = calculate_diameter_from_remaining(reel)
    reel.weight_current_kg = reel.weight_initial_kg * (reel.remaining_pct / 100)
Cálculo de diámetro desde remaining
def calculate_diameter_from_remaining(reel):
    # Diámetro decrece según remaining %
    # Asumiendo paper thickness constante
    paper_thickness_mm = 0.2  # típico
    initial_outer_diameter = reel.diameter_initial_mm
    initial_core_diameter = 100  # mm
    
    # Capas consumidas
    total_length_consumed_m = reel.length_consumed_m
    layers_consumed = total_length_consumed_m / (reel.width_mm / 1000)  # simplificado
    
    # Nuevo diámetro externo
    new_diameter = initial_core_diameter + 2 * (initial_outer_diameter/2 - initial_core_diameter/2) * (reel.remaining_pct / 100)
    return max(new_diameter, initial_core_diameter)
Cálculo de paper consumption
def calculate_paper_consumed_kg(reel, meters):
    # kg = m × gramage (g/m²) × width (m) / 1000
    paper_grade = get_paper_grade(reel.paper_grade_id)
    kg = meters * paper_grade.gramage * (reel.width_mm / 1000) / 1000
    return kg
Parámetros de Configuración
# config_reel.yaml
reel:
  name: "Reel Configuration"
  category: "entity"
  
  dimensions:
    diameter_max_mm: 1500
    diameter_avg_mm: 1250
    diameter_min_mm: 850
    width_avg_mm: 2500
    width_min_mm: 1800
    width_max_mm: 3500
    
  weight:
    weight_avg_kg: 2100
    weight_min_kg: 800
    weight_max_kg: 3500
    
  length:
    length_avg_m: 12000
    length_min_m: 5000
    length_max_m: 25000
    length_distribution: "normal"
    
  consumption:
    remaining_pct_at_return_avg: 18
    remaining_pct_threshold_for_return: 5
    min_diameter_for_use_mm: 200
    
  quality:
    damaged_probability_pct: 0.2
    wrong_grade_probability_pct: 0.5
    quality_grades: ["A", "B", "C"]
    quality_distribution:
      "A": 0.85
      "B": 0.13
      "C": 0.02
      
  rfid:
    enabled: true
    encoding: "EPC_GEN2"
    read_range_m: 5
    write_capability: true
    
  cost:
    avg_cost_eur: 1200
    cost_min_eur: 800
    cost_max_eur: 2000
    cost_by_quality_grade:
      "A": 1.2
      "B": 1.0
      "C": 0.7
      
  validation:
    cross_parameter_rules:
      - rule: "diameter_min < diameter_avg < diameter_max"
      - rule: "weight_min < weight_avg < weight_max"
      - rule: "length_remaining >= 0"
      - rule: "remaining_pct between 0 AND 100"
      - rule: "sum(quality_distribution) == 1.0"
      
  kpi_impacted:
    - "reel_changes_per_h"
    - "reel_returns_per_h"
    - "remaining_pct_at_return"
    - "paper_consumed_kg_per_h"
    - "wrong_reel_events_count"
    - "damaged_reel_events_count"
    - "quality_rate_pct"
    - "LPI"
    
  risk: "bajo"
  priority: "crítica"
Reglas de Validación
R1: diameter_current ≥ 0
R2: length_consumed + length_remaining == length_initial
R3: remaining_pct == (length_remaining / length_initial) × 100
R4: weight_current == weight_initial × (remaining_pct / 100)
R5: Si status == IN_USE → location == RollStand
R6: Si status == ON_TRACK → location == Track
R7: Si status == IN_WAREHOUSE → location == Warehouse
R8: paper_grade_id consistente durante todo el lifecycle
KPIs generados
KPI	Fórmula	Frecuencia
Reels Consumed/h	count / hours	Continuo
Reels Returned/h	count / hours	Continuo
Avg Remaining % at Return	mean(remaining_pct)	Por turno
Paper Consumed kg/h	sum(kg) / hours	Continuo
Quality Rate %	good / total	Continuo
Avg Reel Lifetime (h)	mean(creation_to_consumed)	Diario
Damage Rate %	damaged / total	Diario
Algoritmos relacionados
algo_02_reel_allocation.md → asignación
algo_03_warehouse_selection.md → selección de origen
algo_13_oee_calculation.md → contribution a quality
Riesgos específicos
Riesgo	Probabilidad	Impacto	Mitigación
Daño físico	Baja (0.2%)	Medio	Manejo cuidadoso + velocidad limitada
Paper grade incorrecta	Baja (0.5%)	Alto	RFID verification
Remaining < threshold	Media	Bajo	Retorno automático
RFID no leído	Baja	Medio	Lectura redundante
Stock-out	Baja	Crítico	Replenishment policy
Estados resumidos para quick reference
Estado	Ubicación típica	Transición siguiente
IN_WAREHOUSE	Warehouse slot	ALLOCATED
ALLOCATED	Warehouse (reservado)	IN_TRANSIT
IN_TRANSIT	Forklift/Transfer	AT_EXCHANGE
AT_EXCHANGE	Exchange zone	ON_TRACK
ON_TRACK	Track (esperando)	IN_USE
IN_USE	RollStand (consumiendo)	RETURN_REQUESTED
RETURN_REQUESTED	Track (esperando return)	IN_RETURN
IN_RETURN	Forklift/Transfer	IN_WAREHOUSE
WRONG_REEL	Cualquiera	SCRAPPED
DAMAGED	Cualquiera	SCRAPPED
CONSUMED	N/A	END
SCRAPPED	Reciclaje	END
Prioridad de desarrollo
Crítica — Entidad central de toda la simulación.

# 📄 ARCHIVO 6: `02_SIMULATION_MODEL/11_ProductionOrder.md`

```markdown
# 11 – Production Order
# INGETRANS Reel Loading Simulator V4

## Propósito
Entidad de negocio que representa una orden de fabricación de cartón corrugado. Tiene longitud objetivo, paper grade requerida, prioridad y fecha de entrega. Es el driver principal del consumo de reels y, por tanto, del flujo logístico completo.

## Entradas
- Órdenes del ERP/MES del cliente
- Calendar (planning semanal/diario)
- Demandas urgentes (rush orders)
- Estado de la corrugadora

## Salidas
- Consumo de metros lineales (a corrugadora)
- Consumo de reels
- Estado de la orden (pending/in_progress/completed)
- Tiempo de ciclo de la orden
- Lead time vs due date

## Configuración
Ver `03_CONFIG_DATABASE/config_production.yaml`

## Dependencias
- Depende de: PaperGrade, Corrugator, Reel
- Consumida por: Logistics Engine, Production Engine, KPI Engine, Financial Engine

## Validación
- length ∈ [min, max]
- priority ∈ {low, normal, high, urgent}
- status transiciones válidas
- paper_grade_id válido

## KPIs afectados
- Order Cycle Time
- On-Time Delivery %
- Order Lead Time
- Production Real vs Target
- Urgent Orders Count
- Order Mix Distribution

## Riesgo
- **Bajo**: entidad pasiva, solo es trackeada

## Prioridad
- **Alta**

---

## Atributos

| Atributo | Tipo | Unidad | Default | Min | Max | Obligatorio |
|---|---|---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| order_id | str | - | "PO-XXXXX" | - | - | Sí |
| customer_id | str | - | "CUST-01" | - | - | Sí |
| paper_grade_id | str | - | "PG-01" | - | - | Sí |
| length_target_m | float | m | 1100 | 150 | 8000 | Sí |
| length_produced_m | float | m | 0 | 0 | length_target | Sí |
| length_remaining_m | float | m | 1100 | 0 | 8000 | Sí |
| width_mm | float | mm | 2500 | 1800 | 3500 | Sí |
| priority | str | - | "normal" | - | - | Sí |
| status | str | - | "pending" | - | - | Sí |
| creation_ts | timestamp | s | 0 | - | - | Sí |
| start_ts | timestamp | s | 0 | - | - | No |
| due_ts | timestamp | s | 0 | - | - | Sí |
| completion_ts | timestamp | s | 0 | - | - | No |
| num_reels_used | int | Nº | 0 | 0 | 100 | Sí |
| quality_pass | bool | - | true | - | - | Sí |
| cost_target_eur | float | € | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| cost_actual_eur | float | € | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |

---

## Estados (State Machine)

PENDING → ALLOCATED → IN_PROGRESS → COMPLETED ↓ PAUSED → IN_PROGRESS ↓ CANCELLED → END


### Transiciones
| Desde | Evento | Hacia | Condición |
|---|---|---|---|
| PENDING | resources_ready | ALLOCATED | reels + stand disponibles |
| ALLOCATED | corrugator_start | IN_PROGRESS | - |
| IN_PROGRESS | target_reached | COMPLETED | produced >= target |
| IN_PROGRESS | paused | PAUSED | manual o failure |
| PAUSED | resumed | IN_PROGRESS | - |
| * | cancelled | CANCELLED | admin action |

---

## Inputs
1. **Nueva orden** desde ERP → ORDER_CREATED
2. **Planificación** desde scheduler → ORDER_SCHEDULED
3. **Rush order** → URGENT_FLAG
4. **Recursos disponibles** → ORDER_ALLOCATED
5. **Inicio de producción** → ORDER_STARTED
6. **Cancelación** desde admin → ORDER_CANCELLED

## Outputs
1. **Eventos**: ORDER_CREATED, ORDER_ALLOCATED, ORDER_STARTED, ORDER_COMPLETED, ORDER_CANCELLED
2. **Producción incremental** (m/segundo)
3. **Consumo de reels** (reel_id usados)
4. **Métricas**: cycle time, lead time, on-time
5. **Costes** (target vs actual)

---

## Relaciones
ProductionOrder (N) ───- pertenece_a ──── (1) Customer ProductionOrder (1) ───- usa ──── (1) PaperGrade ProductionOrder (1) ───- ejecutado_por ──── (1) Corrugator ProductionOrder (1) ───- consume ──── (N) Reel ProductionOrder (1) ───- mide ──── (1) KPIEngine ProductionOrder (1) ───- genera ──── (1) Revenue


---

## Lifecycle

### Fase 1: Creación (PENDING)
- Recibida del ERP con paper_grade + length + due_date
- Validación de viabilidad
- Asignación de prioridad

### Fase 2: Asignación (ALLOCATED)
- Scheduler asigna corrugator
- Logística reserva reels en warehouse
- Pre-asignación de roll stands

### Fase 3: Ejecución (IN_PROGRESS)
- Corrugador inicia producción
- Consumo continuo de metros
- Reels reemplazados según necesidad
- Tracking de producción parcial

### Fase 4: Completado (COMPLETED)
- Longitud target alcanzada
- Cálculo de cycle time
- Cálculo de on-time delivery
- Snapshot final (reels usados, costes, calidad)

---

## Algoritmos de cálculo

### Estimación de número de reels necesarios
```python
def estimate_reels_needed(order_length_m, paper_grade, reel_length_avg=12000):
    # Asumiendo length_avg de 12,000 m por reel
    reels_needed = math.ceil(order_length_m / reel_length_avg)
    # + 10% buffer para remaining al final
    reels_needed = int(reels_needed * 1.10)
    return reels_needed
Cálculo de tiempo de ciclo estimado
def estimate_cycle_time(order_length_m, corrugator_speed_avg=220):
    # Tiempo = longitud / velocidad
    # En minutos
    time_min = order_length_m / corrugator_speed_avg
    # En horas
    time_h = time_min / 60
    return time_h
Cálculo de lead time
def calculate_lead_time(order):
    if order.completion_ts and order.due_ts:
        lead_time_s = order.due_ts - order.completion_ts
        on_time = lead_time_s >= 0
        return lead_time_s, on_time
Asignación de prioridad
def assign_priority(order, urgent_queue_length):
    # Si hay pocas urgentes, marcar como urgent
    if order.due_ts - current_time < 4 * 3600:  # < 4 horas
        return "urgent"
    elif order.due_ts - current_time < 24 * 3600:  # < 24 horas
        return "high"
    else:
        return "normal"
Distribución de órdenes (Typical European Plant)
Tipo	Rango de longitud	Ratio	Avg length (m)
Short	< 500 m	35%	350
Medium	500-1,500 m	45%	1,000
Long	> 1,500 m	20%	3,000
Urgent	cualquiera	3/turno	variable
Distribución estadística (empírica)
# Distribución por tramos
if random() < 0.35:
    length = uniform(150, 500)  # short
elif random() < 0.80:
    length = uniform(500, 1500)  # medium
else:
    length = uniform(1500, 8000)  # long
Parámetros de Configuración
# config_production.yaml
production_order:
  name: "Production Order Configuration"
  category: "business_entity"
  
  dimensions:
    length_min_m: 150
    length_avg_m: 1100
    length_max_m: 8000
    length_distribution: "empirical"
    
  mix:
    short_orders_pct: 35
    medium_orders_pct: 45
    long_orders_pct: 20
    urgent_orders_per_shift: 3
    
  priority:
    levels: ["low", "normal", "high", "urgent"]
    default: "normal"
    urgent_max_per_day: 10
    urgent_handling: "preempt_normal"
    
  scheduling:
    strategy: "edd"  # earliest due date
    buffer_time_min: 15  # margen entre órdenes
    lookahead_h: 8  # planificar próximas 8h
    
  quality:
    pass_rate_pct: 99.0
    rework_allowed: true
    scrap_threshold_pct: 1.0
    
  cost:
    revenue_per_m_eur: 0.85
    cost_per_m_eur: 0.45
    margin_pct: 47
    
  validation:
    cross_parameter_rules:
      - rule: "length_min < length_avg < length_max"
      - rule: "short_pct + medium_pct + long_pct == 100"
      - rule: "urgent_orders_per_shift >= 0"
      - rule: "pass_rate_pct > 95"
      
  kpi_impacted:
    - "order_cycle_time_h"
    - "on_time_delivery_pct"
    - "lead_time_h"
    - "production_real_vs_target_pct"
    - "urgent_orders_count"
    - "revenue_eur_per_year"
    - "LPI"
    
  risk: "bajo"
  priority: "alta"
Reglas de Validación
R1: length_min ≤ length_target ≤ length_max
R2: length_produced + length_remaining == length_target
R3: priority ∈ {low, normal, high, urgent}
R4: status transiciones válidas
R5: Si status == COMPLETED → completion_ts > start_ts
R6: num_reels_used ≥ 1 si status == COMPLETED
R7: paper_grade_id debe existir en catálogo
KPIs generados
KPI	Fórmula	Frecuencia
Order Cycle Time (h)	completion_ts - start_ts	Por orden
On-Time Delivery %	count(on_time) / total	Diario
Lead Time (h)	due_ts - completion_ts	Por orden
Avg Order Length (m)	mean(length_target)	Diario
Urgent Orders Count	count(priority==urgent)	Diario
Order Completion Rate	completed / received	Diario
Production Target Achievement	produced / target	Por orden
Algoritmos relacionados
algo_01_order_generation.md → generación de órdenes
algo_07_priority_management.md → gestión de prioridades
algo_13_oee_calculation.md → contribution a OEE
Riesgos específicos
Riesgo	Probabilidad	Impacto	Mitigación
Orden no completada a tiempo	Media	Alto	EDD scheduling + buffer
Cancelación tardía	Baja	Medio	Pre-allocation flexible
Urgent excessive	Baja	Alto	Límite 10/día + priorización
Cambio de paper grade	Baja	Alto	Validación + reasignación
Reel shortage	Baja	Crítico	Buffer de stock
Comparativa del impacto en Forklift vs INGETRANS
Métrica	Forklift (A)	INGETRANS (B)	Mejora
On-Time Delivery	88%	96%	+8 pp
Order Cycle Time (avg)	6.5 h	5.2 h	-20%
Lead Time médio	1.8 h	0.5 h	-72%
Urgent completion rate	92%	99%	+7 pp
Customer satisfaction	85%	95%	+10 pp
Prioridad de desarrollo
Alta — Driver del sistema completo.

📄 ARCHIVO 1: 02_SIMULATION_MODEL/12_PaperGrade.md
# 12 – Paper Grade
# INGETRANS Reel Loading Simulator V4

## Propósito
Catálogo de los 18 tipos de papel que gestiona la planta. Define las propiedades técnicas de cada grado (gramaje, ancho, tipo, color, proveedor) que condicionan el consumo, los costes y la asignación a roll stands y órdenes de producción.

## Entradas
- Especificaciones técnicas del proveedor
- Demandas desde Production Orders
- Asignación desde Roll Stands
- Stock en warehouse

## Salidas
- Catálogo de grados disponibles
- Stock por grado
- Consumo por grado
- Precio por grado
- Propiedades físicas (para simulación)

## Configuración
Ver `03_CONFIG_DATABASE/config_paper_grade.yaml`

## Dependencias
- Depende de: Warehouse (stock), Reel (atributos)
- Consumida por: ProductionOrder, RollStand, Corrugator, Reel

## Validación
- 18 grados definidos exactamente
- gramaje ∈ [60, 400] g/m²
- ancho ∈ [1800, 3500] mm
- precio > 0

## KPIs afectados
- Stock por grado
- Consumo por grado (kg/h)
- Coste por grado
- Quality rate por grado
- Order mix por grado

## Riesgo
- **Bajo**: catálogo estático, cambia solo en reconfiguración

## Prioridad
- **Alta**

---

## Atributos

| Atributo | Tipo | Unidad | Default | Min | Max | Obligatorio |
|---|---|---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| paper_grade_id | str | - | "PG-01" | - | - | Sí |
| name | str | - | "Kraftliner 175" | - | - | Sí |
| type | str | - | "kraftliner" | - | - | Sí |
| category | str | - | "liner" | - | - | Sí |
| gramage_g_m2 | float | g/m² | 175 | 60 | 400 | Sí |
| width_min_mm | float | mm | 2400 | 1800 | 3500 | Sí |
| width_max_mm | float | mm | 2800 | 1800 | 3500 | Sí |
| width_std_mm | float | mm | 2500 | 1800 | 3500 | Sí |
| color | str | - | "brown" | - | - | Sí |
| supplier_id | str | - | "SUP-01" | - | - | Sí |
| cost_eur_per_kg | float | €/kg | 0.95 | 0.5 | 2.5 | Sí |
| stock_current_kg | float | kg | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |
| stock_min_kg | float | kg | 1000 | 0 | - | Sí |
| stock_max_kg | float | kg | 20000 | 0 | - | Sí |
| consumption_rate_kg_per_h | float | kg/h | 0 | 0 | - | No |
| quality_grade_default | str | - | "A" | - | - | Sí |
| burst_strength_kpa | float | kPa | 350 | 100 | 800 | Sí |
| thickness_mm | float | mm | 0.25 | 0.1 | 0.6 | Sí |
| moisture_pct | float | % | 8 | 4 | 12 | Sí |
| recyclability_pct | float | % | 100 | 0 | 100 | Sí |
| fsc_certified | bool | - | true | - | - | Sí |

---

## Estados (State Machine)

AVAILABLE → LOW_STOCK → OUT_OF_STOCK → REORDERED → AVAILABLE ↓ DISCONTINUED (rare)


### Transiciones
| Desde | Evento | Hacia | Condición |
|---|---|---|---|
| AVAILABLE | stock_check | LOW_STOCK | stock < min_level |
| LOW_STOCK | stock_check | OUT_OF_STOCK | stock == 0 |
| OUT_OF_STOCK | reorder_triggered | REORDERED | - |
| REORDERED | delivery_received | AVAILABLE | stock >= min_level |
| AVAILABLE | stock_updated | LOW_STOCK | - |
| * | admin_action | DISCONTINUED | manual |

---

## Inputs
1. Replenishment orders → stock_updated
2. Consumption desde Corrugator → stock_decremented
3. Quality inspection → quality_grade_updated
4. Admin actions → grade_discontinued

## Outputs
1. Stock snapshot por grado
2. Consumption rate por grado
3. Cost accumulation
4. Low stock alerts
5. Quality metrics

---

## Relaciones
PaperGrade (1) ───- clasifica ──── (N) Reel PaperGrade (1) ───- usado_por ──── (N) ProductionOrder PaperGrade (1) ───- asignado_a ──── (N) RollStand PaperGrade (1) ───- consumido_por ──── (1) Corrugator PaperGrade (1) ───- suministrado_por ──── (1) Supplier PaperGrade (1) ───- mide ──── (1) KPIEngine

## Algoritmos de cálculo

### Estimación de consumo por grado
```python
def calculate_consumption(grade, production_m):
    # kg = m × gramage × width / 1e6
    kg = production_m * grade.gramage * (grade.width_std / 1000) / 1000
    return kg
Coste de consumo
def calculate_cost(grade, kg_consumed):
    return kg_consumed * grade.cost_eur_per_kg
Tiempo de vida del stock
def calculate_stock_lifetime_h(grade):
    if grade.consumption_rate_kg_per_h > 0:
        return grade.stock_current_kg / grade.consumption_rate_kg_per_h
    return float('inf')
Trigger de reorder
def should_reorder(grade):
    return grade.stock_current_kg < grade.stock_min_kg
Parámetros de Configuración

R3: cost_eur_kg > 0
R4: stock_min_kg < stock_max_kg
R5: width_min ≤ width_std ≤ width_max
R6: sum(usage_distribution) == 100
R7: Todos los IDs únicos
R8: Todos los grados tienen al menos 1 proveedor
KPIs generados
KPI	Fórmula	Frecuencia
Stock por grado (kg)	current	Continuo
Consumption por grado (kg/h)	consumption / hours	Continuo
Cost por grado (€/h)	kg × cost_eur_kg	Continuo
Stock lifetime (h)	stock / consumption_rate	Continuo
Reorder frequency	count(reorders)	Diario
Quality rate por grado	good / total	Diario

algo_02_reel_allocation.md → asignación por paper grade
algo_01_order_generation.md → selección de grade por orden
Riesgos específicos
Riesgo	Probabilidad	Impacto	Mitigación
Stock-out de grado crítico	Baja	Crítico	Min stock levels + alertas
Sobrestock	Media	Bajo	Max stock levels
Cambio de proveedor	Baja	Medio	Multi-sourcing
Calidad degradada	Baja	Medio	Inspección incoming
Discontinuación	Muy baja	Alto	Stock de seguridad
Asignación típica a planta de 5 stands
RS-01: Kraftliner 175 (liner principal externo)
RS-02: Kraftliner 200 (liner principal interno)
RS-03: Testliner 140 (liner secundario)
RS-04: Fluting 112 (fluting medio)
RS-05: Fluting 105 (fluting ligero)
Distribución de uso esperada
Liners (PG-01 a PG-08, PG-16): 60% del consumo
Fluting (PG-09 a PG-13):      33% del consumo
Specialty (PG-14, PG-15):      4% del consumo
Premium (PG-17, PG-18):         3% del consumo
Prioridad de desarrollo
Alta — Define el catálogo de materiales de la planta.

# 📄 ARCHIVO 2: `02_SIMULATION_MODEL/13_Shift.md`

```markdown
# 13 – Shift
# INGETRANS Reel Loading Simulator V4

## Propósito
Define los turnos de trabajo, breaks, holidays y calendario operativo de la planta. Es el driver temporal de eventos como shift changes, breaks, ausencias y ventanas de mantenimiento.

## Entradas
- Calendar corporativo
- Acuerdos laborales
- Demandas de producción
- Ventanas de mantenimiento

## Salidas
- Shift start/end events
- Break start/end events
- Shift change overhead events
- Working time calculation

## Configuración
Ver `03_CONFIG_DATABASE/config_shift.yaml`

## Dependencias
- Depende de: SimulationClock, Calendar
- Consumida por: Operator, Forklift, Corrugator, Maintenance, KPI Engine

## Validación
- shifts cubren 24h sin solapamiento
- breaks dentro de shifts
- shift_change_delay > 0
- work_days válidos

## KPIs afectados
- Availability (shift_time vs total_time)
- Operator productivity
- Shift change overhead
- Labor cost

## Riesgo
- **Bajo**: configuración estable

## Prioridad
- **Alta**

---

## Atributos

| Atributo | Tipo | Unidad | Default | Min | Max | Obligatorio |
|---|---|---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| shift_id | str | - | "S-DAY" | - | - | Sí |
| name | str | - | "Day Shift" | - | - | Sí |
| start_time | time | HH:MM | "06:00" | - | - | Sí |
| end_time | time | HH:MM | "14:00" | - | - | Sí |
| duration_h | float | h | 8.0 | 4.0 | 12.0 | Sí |
| num_operators | int | Nº | 1 | 0 | 10 | Sí |
| num_forklifts | int | Nº | 1 | 0 | 5 | Sí |
| shift_change_delay_min | float | min | 5 | 0 | 30 | Sí |
| breaks | list | - | [] | - | - | Sí |
| work_days | list | - | [mon-fri] | - | - | Sí |
| cost_multiplier | float | 1.0 | 1.0 | 0.5 | 2.0 | Sí |
| active | bool | - | true | - | - | Sí |

---

## Estados (State Machine)

SCHEDULED → ACTIVE → BREAK → ACTIVE → ENDED ↓ PAUSED → ACTIVE ↓ HOLIDAY (no operativo)


### Transiciones
| Desde | Evento | Hacia | Condición |
|---|---|---|---|
| SCHEDULED | time_reached | ACTIVE | time == start_time |
| ACTIVE | break_time | BREAK | time == break.start |
| BREAK | break_end | ACTIVE | time == break.end |
| ACTIVE | time_reached | ENDED | time == end_time |
| ACTIVE | pause_signal | PAUSED | - |
| PAUSED | resume_signal | ACTIVE | - |
| * | holiday_active | HOLIDAY | date in holidays |

---

## Inputs
1. Calendar corporativo
2. Holiday list
3. Maintenance windows
4. Operator availability
5. Production demand

## Outputs
1. SHIFT_START event
2. SHIFT_END event
3. BREAK_START event
4. BREAK_END event
5. SHIFT_CHANGE event
6. Working time metrics

---

## Relaciones
Shift (1) ───- asignado_a ──── (N) Operator Shift (1) ───- opera ──── (N) Forklift Shift (1) ───- consume ──── (1) Corrugator Shift (1) ───- permite ──── (N) Maintenance Shift (1) ───- mide ──── (1) KPIEngine Shift (1) ───- genera_costes ──── (1) FinancialEngine


---

## Configuración de Turnos Típica (2 shifts/día)

### Shift 1: Día (S-DAY)
Inicio: 06:00 Fin: 14:00 Duración: 8 horas Operadores: 1 Forklifts: 1 Breaks:

Break 1: 10:00 - 10:15 (15 min)
Break 2: 12:00 - 12:15 (15 min) Total breaks: 30 min Tiempo efectivo: 7.5 h Cost multiplier: 1.0

### Shift 2: Tarde (S-NIGHT)
Inicio: 14:00 Fin: 22:00 Duración: 8 horas Operadores: 1 (distinto) Forklifts: 1 (mismo, handoff) Breaks:

Break 1: 16:00 - 16:15
Break 2: 19:00 - 19:15 Total breaks: 30 min Tiempo efectivo: 7.5 h Cost multiplier: 1.25 (night shift)

### Shift 3: Noche (S-LATE) [Opcional]
Inicio: 22:00 Fin: 06:00 Duración: 8 horas Operadores: 0 (no supervisado) Forklifts: 0 (solo INGETRANS) Breaks: N/A Tiempo efectivo: 8 h Cost multiplier: 1.35 (late night)


---

## Algoritmos de cálculo

### Working time por turno
```python
def calculate_working_time(shift):
    total_min = shift.duration_h * 60
    breaks_min = sum(b.duration_min for b in shift.breaks)
    shift_change_min = shift.shift_change_delay_min
    return total_min - breaks_min - shift_change_min
Calendar lookup
def is_working_day(date, work_days):
    weekday = date.strftime("%a").lower()
    return weekday in work_days
Shift assignment
def get_current_shift(current_time, shifts_today):
    for shift in shifts_today:
        if shift.start_time <= current_time < shift.end_time:
            return shift
    return None
Parámetros de Configuración
# config_shift.yaml
shift:
  name: "Shift Configuration"
  category: "calendar"
  
  total_shifts_per_day: 2
  total_hours_per_day: 16  # 06:00 - 22:00
  total_hours_per_year: 5280  # 330 días × 16h
  
  shifts:
    - shift_id: "S-DAY"
      name: "Day Shift"
      start_time: "06:00"
      end_time: "14:00"
      duration_h: 8.0
      num_operators: 1
      num_forklifts: 1
      cost_multiplier: 1.0
      shift_change_delay_min: 5
      breaks:
        - start: "10:00"
          end: "10:15"
          duration_min: 15
          type: "coffee"
        - start: "12:00"
          end: "12:15"
          duration_min: 15
          type: "lunch_partial"
      active: true
      
    - shift_id: "S-NIGHT"
      name: "Evening Shift"
      start_time: "14:00"
      end_time: "22:00"
      duration_h: 8.0
      num_operators: 1
      num_forklifts: 1
      cost_multiplier: 1.25
      shift_change_delay_min: 5
      breaks:
        - start: "16:00"
          end: "16:15"
          duration_min: 15
          type: "coffee"
        - start: "19:00"
          end: "19:15"
          duration_min: 15
          type: "dinner_partial"
      active: true
      
  work_days:
    - "mon"
    - "tue"
    - "wed"
    - "thu"
    - "fri"
    # "sat" opcional
    # "sun" opcional (normalmente no)
    
  holidays:
    - "2024-01-01"  # Año Nuevo
    - "2024-01-06"  # Reyes
    - "2024-05-01"  # Día del Trabajo
    - "2024-08-15"  # Asunción
    - "2024-10-12"  # Hispanidad
    - "2024-11-01"  # Todos los Santos
    - "2024-12-06"  # Constitución
    - "2024-12-08"  # Inmaculada
    - "2024-12-25"  # Navidad
    
  overtime:
    enabled: false
    max_hours_per_week: 48
    cost_multiplier: 1.5
    auto_trigger_pct: 95  # % target production
    
  maintenance_windows:
    - day: "sun"
      start_time: "02:00"
      end_time: "06:00"
      type: "preventive"
      recurring: "weekly"
      
  validation:
    cross_parameter_rules:
      - rule: "shifts do not overlap"
      - rule: "breaks within shift duration"
      - rule: "num_operators <= num_forklifts"
      - rule: "shift_change_delay < break_duration"
      - rule: "all(break.duration_min > 0)"
      
  kpi_impacted:
    - "availability_pct"
    - "operator_productivity_reels_per_h"
    - "labor_cost_eur_per_year"
    - "shift_change_overhead_min_per_day"
    - "effective_working_time_h_per_day"
    
  risk: "bajo"
  priority: "alta"
Reglas de Validación
R1: Shifts no se solapan
R2: Breaks dentro del shift
R3: num_operators <= num_forklifts (asignación 1:1)
R4: Holidays son fechas válidas
R5: shift_change_delay < 30 min
R6: Working days ∈ {mon, tue, wed, thu, fri, sat, sun}
KPIs generados
KPI	Fórmula	Frecuencia
Effective Working Time (h)	shift_duration - breaks	Diario
Shift Change Overhead (min)	sum(shift_change_delay)	Diario
Labor Cost per Shift (€)	hours × cost × multiplier	Diario
Operator Productivity	reels / hours_active	Por turno
Overtime Hours	sum(overtime)	Semanal
Working Days per Year	365 - holidays - weekends	Anual
Cálculo de horas efectivas anuales
Total horas/año: 8,760 (365 × 24)
- Horas no operativas (22:00 - 06:00): 5,840 h
- Holidays: 9 días × 16h = 144 h
- Weekends: 104 días × 16h = 1,664 h
- Breaks: 220 días × 0.5h × 2 shifts = 220 h
- Shift change: 220 días × 10min × 2 = 73 h

= Horas operativas netas: 819 h
Ajustado a 330 días operativos (Typical European):
330 días × 16h × 2 shifts = 10,560 h brutas
- Breaks: 330 × 0.5h × 2 = 330 h
- Shift change: 330 × 10min × 2 = 110 h

= 10,120 h efectivas/año
Comparativa de turnos Forklift vs INGETRANS
Aspecto	Forklift (2 shifts)	INGETRANS (24/7 opcional)
Horas/día	16 h	24 h
Operadores/día	2	0
Coste laboral/año	246,400 €	0 €
Shift change overhead	110 h/año	0 h
Breaks	330 h/año	0 h
Disponibilidad	92%	97%
Velocidad de cambio	Manual	Continuo 24/7
Algoritmos relacionados
algo_06_forklift_dispatching.md → considera shift del operador
algo_01_order_generation.md → planning por shift
algo_11_maintenance.md → ventanas de mantenimiento
Riesgos específicos
Riesgo	Probabilidad	Impacto	Mitigación
Operador ausente	Baja (1%)	Alto	Backup operator protocol
Shift overrun	Media	Medio	Overtime protocol
Break overrun	Baja	Bajo	Auto-resume
Holiday mal definido	Baja	Bajo	HR validation
Mantenimiento en operativo	Baja	Alto	Maintenance windows
Prioridad de desarrollo
Alta — Define la temporalidad del sistema completo.

# 📄 ARCHIVO 3: `02_SIMULATION_MODEL/14_Maintenance.md`

```markdown
# 14 – Maintenance
# INGETRANS Reel Loading Simulator V4

## Propósito
Proceso de mantenimiento preventivo y correctivo de los equipos (corrugator, transfer, forklift, tracks, roll stands). Modela las paradas planificadas, las reparaciones tras fallos y el impacto en disponibilidad y OEE.

## Entradas
- Maintenance schedule (calendar)
- Failure events (correctivo)
- Equipment runtime (preventivo)
- Crew availability

## Salidas
- MAINTENANCE_START event
- MAINTENANCE_END event
- Equipment downtime
- Maintenance cost
- Updated MTBF/MTTR

## Configuración
Ver `03_CONFIG_DATABASE/config_maintenance.yaml`

## Dependencias
- Depende de: Corrugator, Forklift, AutomaticTransfer, Shift, Failure
- Consumida por: Simulation Engine, KPI Engine, Financial Engine

## Validación
- maintenance intervals > 0
- duration < shift duration
- crew disponible
- equipment en estado válido

## KPIs afectados
- Availability
- OEE
- Downtime %
- Maintenance cost
- MTBF / MTTR
- Failures/month

## Riesgo
- **Alto**: mantenimiento mal programado = pérdida producción

## Prioridad
- **Alta**

---

## Atributos

| Atributo | Tipo | Unidad | Default | Min | Max | Obligatorio |
|---|---|---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| maintenance_id | str | - | "M-XXXX" | - | - | Sí |
| equipment_id | str | - | "CORR-01" | - | - | Sí |
| type | str | - | "preventive" | - | - | Sí |
| scheduled_ts | timestamp | s | 0 | - | - | Sí |
| start_ts | timestamp | s | 0 | - | - | No |
| end_ts | timestamp | s | 0 | - | - | No |
| duration_h | float | h | 4.0 | 0.5 | 72.0 | Sí |
| crew_size | int | Nº | 2 | 1 | 10 | Sí |
| cost_eur | float | € | 500 | 100 | 50000 | Sí |
| status | str | - | "scheduled" | - | - | Sí |
| priority | str | - | "normal" | - | - | Sí |
| description | str | - | "" | - | - | No |
| parts_replaced | list | - | [] | - | - | No |
| next_maintenance_h | float | h | 0 | - | - | No |

---

## Estados (State Machine)

SCHEDULED → IN_PROGRESS → COMPLETED ↓ CANCELLED (admin) ↓ POSTPONED (delay)


### Transiciones
| Desde | Evento | Hacia | Condición |
|---|---|---|---|
| SCHEDULED | time_reached | IN_PROGRESS | - |
| IN_PROGRESS | work_complete | COMPLETED | elapsed >= duration |
| IN_PROGRESS | admin_action | CANCELLED | - |
| SCHEDULED | delay_request | POSTPONED | - |
| POSTPONED | reschedule | SCHEDULED | - |

---

## Tipos de Mantenimiento

### Preventive (Preventivo)
- **Programado**: cada X horas de operación
- **Trigger**: runtime counter o calendar
- **Duración típica**: 4-8h
- **Coste típico**: 500-2,000 €
- **Objetivo**: evitar fallos

### Corrective (Correctivo)
- **No programado**: triggered por failure
- **Trigger**: failure event
- **Duración típica**: 30-90 min (MTTR)
- **Coste típico**: 1,000-10,000 €
- **Objetivo**: restaurar operación

### Predictive (Predictivo)
- **Sensores**: vibación, temperatura, etc.
- **Trigger**: threshold breach
- **Duración**: 2-4h
- **Coste**: 800-1,500 €

### Overhaul (Revisión general)
- **Anual**: cada 8,760h
- **Trigger**: calendar
- **Duración**: 48-72h
- **Coste**: 20,000-50,000 €

---

## Inputs
1. Equipment runtime counter
2. Calendar schedule
3. Failure events
4. Predictive sensor data
5. Crew availability

## Outputs
1. MAINTENANCE_SCHEDULED event
2. MAINTENANCE_STARTED event
3. MAINTENANCE_COMPLETED event
4. Equipment status update (DOWN/UP)
5. Cost accumulation
6. Next maintenance trigger

---

## Relaciones
Maintenance (N) ───- mantiene ──── (1) Equipment Maintenance (1) ───- ejecutado_por ──── (N) CrewMember Maintenance (1) ───- usa ──── (N) SparePart Maintenance (1) ───- genera ──── (1) Cost Maintenance (1) ───- actualiza ──── (1) Equipment [MTBF]


---

## Lifecycle

### Mantenimiento Preventivo
1. Schedule creado (basado en runtime o calendar)
2. Notificación 48h antes
3. Crew asignado + partes preparados
4. Ejecución en ventana de mantenimiento
5. Verificación funcional
6. Update de runtime counter

### Mantenimiento Correctivo
1. Failure detected
2. Crew dispatched
3. Diagnóstico (5-10 min)
4. Reparación
5. Testing
6. Return to service

---

## Algoritmos de scheduling

### Preventive schedule trigger
```python
def should_trigger_pm(equipment, config):
    runtime_since_last = equipment.runtime_h - equipment.last_pm_h
    if runtime_since_last >= config.pm_interval_h:
        return True
    return False
Corrective MTTR sampling
def sample_repair_time(failure_type, mttr_mean, mttr_std):
    return max(5, np.random.normal(mttr_mean, mttr_std))
Maintenance window validation
def is_valid_window(start_ts, shift_calendar):
    # Verificar que está en ventana permitida
    if is_holiday(start_ts): return False
    if is_outside_shift(start_ts): return False
    return True
Parámetros de Configuración

Reglas de Validación
R1: pm_interval_h > 0
R2: duration_h < 24 (no más de 1 día)
R3: crew_size >= 1
R4: Maintenance window dentro de shift permitido
R5: events_per_month <= 30 (sanity check)
R6: cost_eur > 0
KPIs generados
KPI	Fórmula	Frecuencia
Maintenance Hours/year	sum(durations)	Anual
Maintenance Cost €/year	sum(costs)	Anual
PM Compliance %	pm_done / pm_scheduled	Mensual
CM Response Time	avg(repair_start - failure)	Mensual
Overdue PMs	count(runtime > interval)	Diario
Spare Parts Stock Value	sum(parts × cost)	Diario
Maintenance Effectiveness	(1 - cm_hours / total_hours)	Mensual
Cálculo de disponibilidad
Availability = (PlannedTime - DownTime) / PlannedTime

DownTime = PM_downtime + CM_downtime + Setup_downtime

PM_downtime = 2 events/month × 6 h/event × 12 months = 144 h/year
CM_downtime = 6 failures/month × 0.75 h/failure × 12 months = 54 h/year
Setup_downtime = 4 cambios/día × 5 min × 220 días = 73 h/year
Total DownTime = 271 h/year

PlannedTime = 5,280 h/year (2 turnos × 220 días × 12 h netas)
Availability = (5,280 - 271) / 5,280 = 94.9%
Comparativa Forklift vs INGETRANS
Aspecto	Forklift	INGETRANS
PM events/month	2	2
PM duration avg	3 h	4 h
CM events/month (failures)	6	3
MTTR	30 min	60 min
Maintenance cost/year	12,000 €	4,000 €
Availability	92%	97%

algo_10_failure_generation.md → trigger correctivo
algo_11_maintenance.md → scheduling preventivo
algo_12_recovery.md → return to service

PM overdue	Media	Alto	Auto-alert + escalación
CM prolongado	Baja	Crítico	Crew de respaldo
Spare part shortage	Baja	Alto	Stock mínimo
Crew unavailable	Baja	Medio	Subcontratación
Overlap con producción	Media	Alto	Maintenance windows
Prioridad de desarrollo
Alta — Crítico para disponibilidad y OEE.

# 📄 ARCHIVO 4: `02_SIMULATION_MODEL/15_Failure.md`

```markdown
# 15 – Failure
# INGETRANS Reel Loading Simulator V4

## Propósito
Modela los eventos de fallo de los equipos (corrugator, transfer, forklift, tracks). Genera paradas no planificadas con distribución estadística (MTBF/MTTR) y diferentes tipos de fallo por equipo.

## Entradas
- Equipment runtime
- Failure distribution (weibull, exponential, lognormal)
- Equipment type
- Operating conditions

## Salidas
- FAILURE_OCCURRED event
- FAILURE_REPAIR_STARTED event

- Cost accumulation

- Depende de: Equipment, Maintenance
- Consumida por: Simulation Engine, KPI Engine, Financial Engine

- MTBF > 0
- MTTR > 0
- sum(failure_types.probability) == 1.0
- distribución válida

- MTTR
- Availability
- OEE
- Failures/month

- **Alta**

|---|---|---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|

| equipment_id | str | - | "CORR-01" | - | - | Sí |
| failure_type | str | - | "unknown" | - | - | Sí |

| occurrence_ts | timestamp | s | 0 | - | - | Sí |

| duration_s | float | s | 0 | 0 | - | Sí |

## Estados (State Machine)

PENDING → DETECTED → REPAIRING → REPAIRED ↓ FALSE_ALARM (rejected)


### Transiciones
| Desde | Evento | Hacia | Condición |
|---|---|---|---|
| PENDING | detection_logic | DETECTED | sensor_threshold_breach |
| DETECTED | crew_dispatched | REPAIRING | - |
| REPAIRING | work_complete | REPAIRED | elapsed >= mttr |
| DETECTED | admin_review | FALSE_ALARM | - |

## Distribución Estadística

### Distribución por equipo

#### Corrugator (MTBF 200h, MTTR 45min)
```python
failure_types = [
    {"type": "belt_tear", "prob": 0.25, "mttr_mean": 30, "mttr_std": 10},
    {"type": "glue_unit", "prob": 0.20, "mttr_mean": 60, "mttr_std": 20},

    {"type": "sensor", "prob": 0.10, "mttr_mean": 20, "mttr_std": 5}
]

    {"type": "tire_damage", "prob": 0.15, "mttr_mean": 60, "mttr_std": 20},

]
distribution = "exponential"
Track (MTBF 2000h, MTTR 120min)
failure_types = [
    {"type": "mechanical_jam", "prob": 0.40, "mttr_mean": 60, "mttr_std": 20},
    {"type": "sensor_fault", "prob": 0.30, "mttr_mean": 30, "mttr_std": 10},
    {"type": "structural", "prob": 0.20, "mttr_mean": 180, "mttr_std": 60},
    {"type": "electrical", "prob": 0.10, "mttr_mean": 45, "mttr_std": 15}
]
distribution = "weibull"
Algoritmos de generación
Sampling time to next failure
def sample_time_to_failure(mtbf_h, distribution="weibull"):
    if distribution == "exponential":
        # TTF = -MTBF * ln(U)
        return -mtbf_h * np.log(np.random.uniform())
    elif distribution == "weibull":
        # TTF = MTBF * (-ln(U))^(1/k)
        k = 2.0  # shape parameter
        return mtbf_h * (-np.log(np.random.uniform()))**(1/k)
    elif distribution == "lognormal":
        # TTF = exp(mu + sigma * Z)
        mu = np.log(mtbf_h) - 0.5
        sigma = 1.0
        return np.exp(mu + sigma * np.random.normal())
Sampling failure type
def sample_failure_type(failure_types):
    r = np.random.uniform()
    cumulative = 0
    for ft in failure_types:
        cumulative += ft["prob"]
        if r < cumulative:
            return ft
    return failure_types[-1]
Sampling MTTR
def sample_mttr(failure_type):
    mttr = max(5, np.random.normal(
        failure_type["mttr_mean"],
        failure_type["mttr_std"]
    ))
    return mttr
Inputs
Equipment runtime counter
Equipment type
Failure distribution config
Sensor data (predictivo)
Operating conditions
Outputs
FAILURE_OCCURRED event
Equipment status → FAILED
Cost event
Downtime tracking
MTTR/MTBF statistics update
Relaciones
Failure (N) ───- afecta ──── (1) Equipment
Failure (1) ───- reparado_por ──── (N) MaintenanceCrew
Failure (1) ───- consume ──── (N) SparePart
Failure (1) ───- genera ──── (1) Cost
Failure (1) ───- actualiza ──── (1) Equipment.MTBF
Failure (1) ───- registra ──── (1) KPIEngine
Lifecycle
Generación: time to next failure sampleado
Detección: sensor threshold breach o alarm
Notificación: alert a maintenance crew
Diagnóstico: 5-10 min para identificar root cause
Reparación: mttr minutos
Testing: 2-5 min de verificación
Return to service: equipment → OPERATIONAL
Post-mortem: root cause analysis (offline)
Parámetros de Configuración

Forklift	80	30	6	12,000 €
AutomaticTransfer	500	60	3	4,000 €
Conclusión: INGETRANS tiene 3x menos fallos y 3x menos coste de mantenimiento.

Algoritmos relacionados
algo_10_failure_generation.md → sampling time to failure
algo_12_recovery.md → return to service
Riesgos específicos
Riesgo	Probabilidad	Impacto	Mitigación
Fallo catastrófico	Muy baja (0.3%)	Crítico	Insurance + backup
Cascada de fallos	Baja	Crítico	Aislamiento por equipo
False alarm	Media	Bajo	Sensor redundancy
Root cause desconocido	Media	Alto	RCM analysis
Recurrencia	Baja	Alto	8D report + CAPA
Prioridad de desarrollo
Alta — Crítico para OEE y disponibilidad.
